<Review>Surprisingly good food, but a bit high on price. The staff were professional and the location is was clean. They specialize in healthier food options focused on salad and kabobs meals, their yogurt dressing is pretty good as well. Decent drink options including the standard sodas, lemonades, teas and a couple others. They have a mini desserts options for the sweet tooth without completely destroying a diet. Expect to pay $ 12+ per plate which is basically a dinner sized portion. As a couple dollars more to add a drinks or dessert and your closer to 15-17$ per person. I would like to eat here more often for the healthier choices as lunch alternatives to fast food, but just to expensive for a regular visit. It would be nice to see more offerings in the $5-7 range with a smaller portion for lunch.

Better that Daphne's, Pita Pita and the Kabab shop.< /Review></record></dataset><record>

<review>I've had Luna Grill before, but only through their catering at events. I found that the chicken breast is always dry so I made sure I skipped it when I went to visit in person.

I'm in a "burger kick" so I looked for a burger and they offer 2. One regular grass-fed beef burger and one vegan alternative.

I ordered the vegan alternative (beyond burger) just to try it and it was alright. I would rate the burger at a low 3 out of 5. It was just okay, it feels like they added it to the menu just to keep up with the trends.

They made it "greek" or mediterranean by adding a  spicy feta cheese dressing, but besides that it feels out of place, it feels lazy and a bit unoriginal.

The service was great, attentive, quick and helpful. 5/5 on that.

Amongst the other dishes, everyone was happy with their dish (except for the chicken). We tried the mahi mahi salad (seasonal salad), chicken & grown sirloin kabobs, and the lemon chicken soup.

The favorite dish by far was the lemon chicken soup, I thought that was amazing and would go back just to get my own bowl. The other favorite was the fries (that seasoning is killer).

Overall, a great experience. But I was right, someone did order the chicken and they found it dry, so unless you like it like that, skip it, and skip the beyond burger until they improve it.< /review>< pictures>

<Review>This is one of my most favorite places to stay.  It is super clean.  Beds are comfortable and linens are soft.  Staff is very friendly and helpful.  They allow dogs at no extra cost!!< /Review><username>Andee Allen< /username>< Pics>

< text>
The hotel room was large (King suite) and the furniture was in very good condition.  The room was bright and inviting.  We stayed in the room for the morning and early afternoon as my wife and I both taught online throughout the day.  The internet held up all three days except for five brief minutes one afternoon.  Mt. Shasta is well worth the visit as there is so much to do outside that you wont be spending too much time indoors during the day.  I dont have much negative to write about our stay except that that the pillows were too firm for my liking.  For breakfast we did the Covid grab a breakfast bag from the hotel office, however I am writing this review from another hotel that is cooking us breakfast and we simply take it to our room so I would have liked that option during our stay at the Strawberry Valley Inn.  With that said, the staff was great, the town was charming and welcoming, and the mountain was truly majestic.  The coffee house Seven Suns made a great everything breakfast sandwich, Sparkys had amazing fire baked pizza, and Yaks on the Five (20 mins south) had the best burger and garlic Parmesan fries that we have ever had.  Try the hiking trail at the end of Ski Lodge street just east of the Sacramento River headwaters near the Sheriffs station for the best views of Mt. Shasta that we found during our stay.  You will see a marker for the trail as you drive up.< /text>

<username>James G< /username><Date>1512339626927< /Date>< Rating>

< review>
What a nice place!
Amazing atmosphere and overall charm.
Breakfast was good and healthy. When we were there they offered coffee, fresh cooked waffles, dry cereal, fresh fruit, dry oatmeal packets, Activia yogurt, OJ and several healthy bread choices.
We were hoping for more of a traditional bacon/sausage/ham and eggs type breakfast.
Although they don't sell wine they do have wine tasting each evening from 5 to 6pm.
Wine is sold across the street at another of their properties.
We stayed in room #1. The bed was way too soft for our liking although some may like it.

We were greeted warmly at the front desk, offered a glass of wine, and she booked a dinner reservation at Lilys as it was 7:30 and the resturant was about to close.  The room was bare bones but clean nad the bed was fine.  The problem was it was 20 degrees outside and the rooms heater was broken (we had not been forwarned about the heat).  A replacement pug in heater was on but not producing heat.  I immediately informed the front desk and was told it would warm up but she would check it while we were at dinner.  We returned close to 9 and no heat or extra blankets.  I again requested heat or blanket.  She had nothing to offer, but made some calls.  By about 9:30 we got a new pug in that fortunately produced adequate heat.  The morning continental breakfast in the front cottage was nice and friendly. All in all the hostess tried pretty hard, but the room was barely adequate.  Wouldnt try again.  We  did get a great price through travel website.< /Text>

< Review>
The Strawberry Valley Inn is under new management since November 2013. The rooms are quiet and clean. There is a continental breakfast at the two smaller, and one larger, table in the main lobby with waffles, boiled eggs, fruit, and decent strong and weak coffee. The new owners are a couple. He fixes things, and she lets you know what is going on in town. There is also a staff, which is very professional. This is a nice quiet place and has a bed and breakfast feel. I would definitely stay here again.<//Review>

< review>
Better than any self wash in California and any carwash I've gone to in Colorado.

Was only in town for a couple of weeks from Colorado and took my car and wife's car (yeah we both drove here) to the Menifee carwash on Newport, since I had been going to them before moving away. Needless to say, I spent $40 for both plus a $10 tip before realizing there were still bugs on our cars and interiors weren't wiped down... A couple days later I took my car to Ramona for a redo before a trip to LA and was surprised that all of the settings worked and that they changed instantly, and the price can't be beat for a self wash. Because of the location to my wife's mother's house, I washed my car at Ramona 3 times a week before leaving. It's a shame we cant get this quality of carwash service in Colorado....< /review>

< Review>
Moved to Corona about 7 months ago and realized I haven't had Chinese since I moved from Whittier CA. So I searched for Chinese fast food and found this spot, came in a little part 8pm on a Friday I asked if they had Tom kha Gai coconut soup the nice employee didn't know so she went to ask in the back, I ordered a combo with broccoli beef and bbq pork then who I believe the owner walks out and the nice lady tells need they don't have coconut soup on the menu because people don't really ask for it but she would make it for me so I go and pay and the owner is just a really nice person would say they would make any custom order.  We had a conversation about the city and welcomed me and my family here so this place deserves 5 stars the coconut soup was delicious the bbq was great as was the broccoli beef, the beef was tender and very flavorful! Thank you!</Review>

< Text>
Tried this place the other night because my wife loves Thai food and saw this place was newly open.  Thai/Chinese food rarely makes it into my top picks just because it doesn't appeal to my taste. That being said, this place has amazing food.  We didn't order from the front pick 'x' items entrees, but rather ordered some of they're prepared fresh items.  I loved their Mongolian Beef and my wife really enjoyed their yellow curry chicken.  Make sure to call ahead if ordering one of their specialty dishes as the wait can be a long time if you order it at the location.  Will be coming back to try some of their other specialties.  As a word of caution, their spicy dishes require that you tell them from 1-10 how spicy you want the dish. I ordered my wife a 6 for the soup (with 10 being the spiciest) and she was barely able to make it thru all the soup. Yet, the great flavor had her work thru the heat till that last drop.< /Text>

Super picky about greasy Chinese food. Most places have MSG generic flavoring and everything kind of melds together in flavor. Not this place. I was pleasantly surprised at how fresh everything was. The only thing fried is the orange chicken.  The portions are generous, the people are friendly and they have an online ordering option they saved us so much time. Our food was hot, vegetables were fresh and had great taste. We had the pad Thai, chicken fried rice, Kung pao (spicy but not burn your mouth off and have no taste kind of Kung Pao) Overall I would recommend this place highly. I didnt feel like people had to roll me out after. Non greasy and well seasoned.< /review>

Weather by the disease or from the medication to treat the disease, my face became more and more gaunt, my cheeks more sunken in, and my facial bones, especially my cheek bones, became very pronounced. I had lipodistrophy. My body  could not maintain or produce healthy facial fat tissue. I was very self conscience of my appearance and it effected my self esteem.
